######################################################################################
#
#l2 multicast route dict defined for vpc and fex l2 multicast sanity
#Per node, IGMP snooping group (*,g)/(s,g) routes are defined in 'snooping_groups' and 
##OMF routes (*,*) are defiend in 'omf_groups'
##igmp_version is optional to be 'v2|v3' and igmp_version='v2' by default; 
##route_type is optional to be 'static|dynamic' and route_type='dynamic' by default;
##If None of source_addr,source_count,source_addr_step is given, only (*,g) will be verified
##For IGMP snooping groups, vlan to oif mapping is always many-to-many mapping.
##For omf_groups, vlan_oif_mapping is optional to be 'one_to_one|many_to_many' and vlan_oif_mapping=many_to_many by default
l2mroute_vpc_dict:
    node01:
        snooping_groups:
            group_range1:
                -vlan_range 5 -group_addr 225.0.0.1 -group_count 1 -group_addr_step 0.0.0.1 -oif_list eth1/5/3,po1,po101 
        omf_groups:
            group_range1:
                -vlan_range 5 -oif_list po101
     
    node02:
        snooping_groups:
            group_range1:
                -vlan_range 5 -group_addr 225.0.0.1 -group_count 1 -group_addr_step 0.0.0.1 -oif_list eth1/5/2,po1,po101 
        omf_groups:
            group_range1:
                -vlan_range 5 -oif_list po101

    node03:
        snooping_groups:
            group_range1:
                -vlan_range 5 -group_addr 225.0.0.1 -group_count 1 -group_addr_step 0.0.0.1 -oif_list eth1/1/1 
        omf_groups:
            group_range1:
                -vlan_range 5 -oif_list po1

            group_range2:
